                      - listitem [ref=e3806]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e3807]:
                          - strong [ref=e3808]: Multi-Timeframe
                          - text: (macro, méso, micro)
                        - list [ref=e3809]:
                          - listitem [ref=e3810]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3811]: "Idem : on a Daily (macro), Hourly (méso) et 5-Minute (micro)."
                          - listitem [ref=e3812]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3813]: "Même architecture : un consolidateur pour le Daily, un pour l’Hourly, un pour 5-Minute."
                      - listitem [ref=e3814]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e3815]:
                          - strong [ref=e3816]: Logique ZigZag + ADX + Trailing Stop
                        - list [ref=e3817]:
                          - listitem [ref=e3818]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3819]:
                              - text: On reprend la même structure de code (classes
                              - code [ref=e3820]: ZigZagCanalDetector
                              - text: ", etc.), en changeant simplement le symbole et quelques ajustements pour la crypto."
                    - separator [ref=e3821]
                    - heading "Code C# Lean" [level=3] [ref=e3822]
                    - generic [ref=e3830]:
                      - generic [ref=e3832]:
                        - generic [ref=e3833]:
                          - img [ref=e3834]
                          - text: C#
                        - button "Copier" [ref=e3837] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - img [ref=e3838]
                      - generic [ref=e3844]:
                        - text: using QuantConnect.Algorithm;
                        - text: using QuantConnect.Data;
                        - text: using QuantConnect.Data.Market;
                        - text: using QuantConnect.Data.Consolidators;
                        - text: using QuantConnect.Indicators;
                        - text: using QuantConnect.Orders;
                        - text: using QuantConnect;
                        - text: using QuantConnect.Brokerages;
                        - text: using System;
                        - text: using System.Collections.Generic;
                        - text: using System.Linq;
                        - text: namespace QuantConnect.Algorithm.CSharp
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: "public class MultiTFBinanceCryptoAlgorithm : QCAlgorithm"
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // ======================
                        - text: // Paramètres Principaux
                        - text: // ======================
                        - text: "private Symbol _symbol; // Paire : BTUSDT (exemple)"
                        - text: private string _ticker = "BTUSDT";
                        - text: // TimeFrames
                        - text: private Resolution _macroResolution = Resolution.Daily;
                        - text: private Resolution _mesoResolution = Resolution.Hour;
                        - text: private TimeSpan _microPeriod = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);
                        - text: // Stockage barres
                        - text: private List<TradeBar> _macroBars;
                        - text: private List<TradeBar> _mesoBars;
                        - text: private List<TradeBar> _microBars;
                        - text: // Détecteurs de canaux
                        - text: private ZigZagCanalDetector _macroDetector;
                        - text: private ZigZagCanalDetector _mesoDetector;
                        - text: private ZigZagCanalDetector _microDetector;
                        - text: // Infos canaux
                        - text: private CanalInfo _macroCanal;
                        - text: private CanalInfo _mesoCanal;
                        - text: private CanalInfo _microCanal;
                        - text: // ADX
                        - text: private AverageDirectionalIndex _adxMacro;
                        - text: private AverageDirectionalIndex _adxMeso;
                        - text: private AverageDirectionalIndex _adxMicro;
                        - text: // Trading
                        - text: private bool _inPosition;
                        - text: private int _positionSize = 10; // Adapté à la crypto
                        - text: private decimal _trailingStop;
                        - text: private decimal _takeProfit1;
                        - text: private decimal _takeProfit2;
                        - text: private bool _partialTaken;
                        - text: public override void Initialize()
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // 1) Configuration Basique
                        - text: SetStartDate(2023, 1, 1);
                        - text: SetEndDate(2023, 7, 1);
                        - text: SetCash(10000);
                        - text: // 2) Brokerage Binance
                        - text: SetBrokerageModel(BrokerageName.Binance, AccountType.Cash);
                        - text: // 3) Benchmark => BTCUSDT
                        - text: "// (ou tout autre symbol, ex: ETHUSDT)"
                        - text: SetBenchmark("BTCUSDT");
                        - text: // 4) Ajout de la crypto qu’on veut trader
                        - text: // On la prend en 'Minute' pour pouvoir consolider en 5-Min & Hour & Daily
                        - text: _symbol = AddCrypto(_ticker, Resolution.Minute, Market.Binance).Symbol;
                        - text: // 5) Listes de stockage des barres
                        - text: _macroBars = new List<TradeBar>();
                        - text: _mesoBars = new List<TradeBar>();
                        - text: _microBars = new List<TradeBar>();
                        - text: // 6) Consolidateurs
                        - text: // === Macro (Daily) ===
                        - text: var macroConsolidator = new TradeBarConsolidator(TimeSpan.FromDays(1));
                        - text: SubscriptionManager.AddConsolidator(_symbol, macroConsolidator);
                        - text: macroConsolidator.DataConsolidated += (sender, bar) =>
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: _macroBars.Add((TradeBar)bar.Clone());
                        - text: if (_macroBars.Count > 2000)
                        - text: _macroBars.RemoveRange(0, _macroBars.Count - 2000);
                        - text: DetectMacroCanal();
                        - text: "};"
                        - text: // === Meso (Hourly) ===
                        - text: var mesoConsolidator = new TradeBarConsolidator(TimeSpan.FromHours(1));
                        - text: SubscriptionManager.AddConsolidator(_symbol, mesoConsolidator);
                        - text: mesoConsolidator.DataConsolidated += (sender, bar) =>
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: _mesoBars.Add((TradeBar)bar.Clone());
                        - text: if (_mesoBars.Count > 2000)
                        - text: _mesoBars.RemoveRange(0, _mesoBars.Count - 2000);
                        - text: DetectMesoCanal();
                        - text: "};"
                        - text: // === Micro (5-Minute) ===
                        - text: var microConsolidator = new TradeBarConsolidator(_microPeriod);
                        - text: SubscriptionManager.AddConsolidator(_symbol, microConsolidator);
                        - text: microConsolidator.DataConsolidated += (sender, bar) =>
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: _microBars.Add((TradeBar)bar.Clone());
                        - text: if (_microBars.Count > 2000)
                        - text: _microBars.RemoveRange(0, _microBars.Count - 2000);
                        - text: DetectMicroCanal();
                        - text: OnMicroBar((TradeBar)bar);
                        - text: "};"
                        - text: // 7) Instanciation ZigZag detectors
                        - text: // threshold = 2% par exemple, minTrendLength=3
                        - text: _macroDetector = new ZigZagCanalDetector(0.02m, 3, "Macro");
                        - text: _mesoDetector = new ZigZagCanalDetector(0.02m, 3, "Meso");
                        - text: _microDetector = new ZigZagCanalDetector(0.02m, 3, "Micro");
                        - text: // 8) ADX
                        - text: _adxMacro = new AverageDirectionalIndex(14);
                        - text: _adxMeso = new AverageDirectionalIndex(14);
                        - text: _adxMicro = new AverageDirectionalIndex(14);
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: public override void OnData(Slice data)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // Logique dans les consolidateurs
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // ===============
                        - text: // DÉTECTION CANAUX
                        - text: // ===============
                        - text: private void DetectMacroCanal()
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: if (_macroBars.Count < 10) return;
                        - text: var lastBar = _macroBars.Last();
                        - text: _adxMacro.Update(lastBar);
                        - text: _macroCanal = _macroDetector.Detect(_macroBars);
                        - text: if (_macroCanal.IsValid &&
                        - text: (_macroCanal.Direction == CanalDirection.Haussier || _macroCanal.Direction == CanalDirection.Baissier) &&
                        - text: _adxMacro.IsReady && _adxMacro.Current.Value < 20)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: _macroCanal.IsValid = false;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: private void DetectMesoCanal()
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: if (_mesoBars.Count < 10) return;
                        - text: var lastBar = _mesoBars.Last();
                        - text: _adxMeso.Update(lastBar);
                        - text: _mesoCanal = _mesoDetector.Detect(_mesoBars);
                        - text: if (_mesoCanal.IsValid &&
                        - text: (_mesoCanal.Direction == CanalDirection.Haussier || _mesoCanal.Direction == CanalDirection.Baissier) &&
                        - text: _adxMeso.IsReady && _adxMeso.Current.Value < 20)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: _mesoCanal.IsValid = false;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: private void DetectMicroCanal()
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: if (_microBars.Count < 10) return;
                        - text: var lastBar = _microBars.Last();
                        - text: _adxMicro.Update(lastBar);
                        - text: _microCanal = _microDetector.Detect(_microBars);
                        - text: if (_microCanal.IsValid &&
                        - text: (_microCanal.Direction == CanalDirection.Haussier || _microCanal.Direction == CanalDirection.Baissier) &&
                        - text: _adxMicro.IsReady && _adxMicro.Current.Value < 20)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: _microCanal.IsValid = false;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // ===============
                        - text: // LOGIQUE TRADING
                        - text: // ===============
                        - text: private void OnMicroBar(TradeBar bar)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: var price = bar.Close;
                        - text: if (_inPosition)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: var holdings = Portfolio[_symbol];
                        - text: // a) Cassure du canal micro ?
                        - text: if (_microCanal.IsValid && _microCanal.IsBroken)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: Liquidate(_symbol, "Micro canal break => exit");
                        - text: _inPosition = false;
                        - text: return;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // b) Trailing Stop
                        - text: if (holdings.IsLong)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // On relève le trailing stop, ex. à (price * 0.995)
                        - text: decimal newStop = price * 0.995m;
                        - text: if (newStop > _trailingStop)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: _trailingStop = newStop;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // Si on retombe en dessous => exit
                        - text: if (price < _trailingStop)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: Liquidate(_symbol, "Trailing Stop triggered (long)");
                        - text: _inPosition = false;
                        - text: return;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // c) Prise de profit partielle
                        - text: if (!_partialTaken && price >= _takeProfit1)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: var half = holdings.Quantity / 2;
                        - text: MarketOrder(_symbol, -half, "Partial TP (long)");
                        - text: _partialTaken = true;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // d) Prise de profit finale
                        - text: if (price >= _takeProfit2)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: Liquidate(_symbol, "Final TP (long)");
                        - text: _inPosition = false;
                        - text: return;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: else if (holdings.IsShort)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // Trailing Stop => on baisse le stop
                        - text: decimal newStop = price * 1.005m;
                        - text: if (newStop < _trailingStop)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: _trailingStop = newStop;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: if (price > _trailingStop)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: Liquidate(_symbol, "Trailing Stop triggered (short)");
                        - text: _inPosition = false;
                        - text: return;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // Partielle
                        - text: if (!_partialTaken && price <= _takeProfit1)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: var half = holdings.Quantity / 2;
                        - text: MarketOrder(_symbol, -half, "Partial TP (short)");
                        - text: _partialTaken = true;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // Finale
                        - text: if (price <= _takeProfit2)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: Liquidate(_symbol, "Final TP (short)");
                        - text: _inPosition = false;
                        - text: return;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: else
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // Pas en position => on check macro, méso, micro
                        - text: if (!_macroCanal.IsValid || !_mesoCanal.IsValid || !_microCanal.IsValid)
                        - text: return;
                        - text: // Ex. haussier
                        - text: if (_macroCanal.Direction == CanalDirection.Haussier &&
                        - text: _mesoCanal.Direction == CanalDirection.Haussier &&
                        - text: _microCanal.Direction == CanalDirection.Haussier)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: MarketOrder(_symbol, +_positionSize, "Micro canal aligned bullish");
                        - text: _inPosition = true;
                        - text: _partialTaken = false;
                        - text: // On fixe un trailingStop initial, ex. 1% sous le prix
                        - text: _trailingStop = price * 0.99m;
                        - text: // On fixe 2 paliers de profit
                        - text: _takeProfit1 = price * 1.01m;
                        - text: _takeProfit2 = price * 1.02m;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // Ex. baissier
                        - text: else if (_macroCanal.Direction == CanalDirection.Baissier &&
                        - text: _mesoCanal.Direction == CanalDirection.Baissier &&
                        - text: _microCanal.Direction == CanalDirection.Baissier)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: MarketOrder(_symbol, -_positionSize, "Micro canal aligned bearish");
                        - text: _inPosition = true;
                        - text: _partialTaken = false;
                        - text: _trailingStop = price * 1.01m;
                        - text: _takeProfit1 = price * 0.99m;
                        - text: _takeProfit2 = price * 0.98m;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "// Range : non implémenté ici"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // ============================
                        - text: // ZIGZAG + CANAL (simplifié)
                        - text: // ============================
                        - text: public class ZigZagCanalDetector
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: private decimal _threshold;
                        - text: private int _minTrendLen;
                        - text: private string _name;
                        - text: private bool _initialized;
                        - text: private decimal _lastPivotPrice;
                        - text: private int _lastPivotIndex;
                        - text: private PivotType _lastPivotType;
                        - text: private bool _directionUp;
                        - text: public ZigZagCanalDetector(decimal thresholdPercent, int minTrendLength, string name)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: _threshold = thresholdPercent;
                        - text: _minTrendLen = minTrendLength;
                        - text: _name = name;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: public CanalInfo Detect(List<TradeBar> bars)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: "var cinfo = new CanalInfo { IsValid = false, Direction = CanalDirection.Unknown };"
                        - text: if (bars.Count < _minTrendLen) return cinfo;
                        - text: var pivots = ComputeZigZagPivots(bars);
                        - text: if (pivots.Count < 2) return cinfo;
                        - text: var lastPivot = pivots.Last();
                        - text: var prevPivot = pivots[pivots.Count - 2];
                        - text: // Logique direction
                        - text: "// Ex: si deux High successifs => haussier si le second est plus haut, etc."
                        - text: if (lastPivot.Type == PivotType.High && prevPivot.Type == PivotType.High)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: if (lastPivot.Price > prevPivot.Price)
                        - text: cinfo.Direction = CanalDirection.Haussier;
                        - text: else
                        - text: cinfo.Direction = CanalDirection.Baissier;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: else if (lastPivot.Type == PivotType.Low && prevPivot.Type == PivotType.Low)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: if (lastPivot.Price < prevPivot.Price)
                        - text: cinfo.Direction = CanalDirection.Baissier;
                        - text: else
                        - text: cinfo.Direction = CanalDirection.Haussier;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: else
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: cinfo.Direction = CanalDirection.Horizontal;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: cinfo.IsValid = true;
                        - text: cinfo.IsBroken = false; // placeholder
                        - text: return cinfo;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // Dans un vrai algo, on testerait la cassure de borne...
                        - text: // On se contente d'un placeholder
                        - text: public bool IsBroken => false;
                        - text: private List<ZigZagPivot> ComputeZigZagPivots(List<TradeBar> bars)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: var pivots = new List<ZigZagPivot>();
                        - text: if (!_initialized)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: _lastPivotIndex = 0;
                        - text: _lastPivotPrice = bars[0].Close;
                        - text: _lastPivotType = PivotType.Low;
                        - text: _directionUp = true;
                        - text: _initialized = true;
                        - text: pivots.Add(new ZigZagPivot(0, PivotType.Low, _lastPivotPrice));
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: for (int i = 1; i < bars.Count; i++)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: var price = bars[i].Close;
                        - text: var variation = (price - _lastPivotPrice) / _lastPivotPrice;
                        - text: if (_directionUp)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: if (price > _lastPivotPrice)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: _lastPivotPrice = price;
                        - text: _lastPivotIndex = i;
                        - text: _lastPivotType = PivotType.High;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: else
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: if (variation < -_threshold)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: pivots.Add(new ZigZagPivot(_lastPivotIndex, PivotType.High, _lastPivotPrice));
                        - text: _directionUp = false;
                        - text: _lastPivotPrice = price;
                        - text: _lastPivotIndex = i;
                        - text: _lastPivotType = PivotType.Low;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: else
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: if (price < _lastPivotPrice)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: _lastPivotPrice = price;
                        - text: _lastPivotIndex = i;
                        - text: _lastPivotType = PivotType.Low;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: else
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: if (variation > _threshold)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: pivots.Add(new ZigZagPivot(_lastPivotIndex, PivotType.Low, _lastPivotPrice));
                        - text: _directionUp = true;
                        - text: _lastPivotPrice = price;
                        - text: _lastPivotIndex = i;
                        - text: _lastPivotType = PivotType.High;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: pivots.Add(new ZigZagPivot(_lastPivotIndex, _lastPivotType, _lastPivotPrice));
                        - text: return pivots;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: public class ZigZagPivot
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: public int Index;
                        - text: public PivotType Type;
                        - text: public decimal Price;
                        - text: public ZigZagPivot(int index, PivotType type, decimal price)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: Index = index;
                        - text: Type = type;
                        - text: Price = price;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: public enum PivotType
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: High,
                        - text: Low
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // Infos canal
                        - text: public class CanalInfo
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: public bool IsValid;
                        - text: public CanalDirection Direction;
                        - text: public bool IsBroken;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: public enum CanalDirection
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: Unknown,
                        - text: Haussier,
                        - text: Baissier,
                        - text: Horizontal
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                    - heading "Commentaires et Points d’attention" [level=3] [ref=e3845]
                    - list [ref=e3846]:
                      - listitem [ref=e3847]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e3848]:
                          - strong [ref=e3849]: Paire Fictive “BTUSDT”
                        - list [ref=e3850]:
                          - listitem [ref=e3851]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3852]:
                              - text: Remplacez par la paire réelle que vous souhaitez, ex.
                              - strong [ref=e3853]:
                                - code [ref=e3854]: BTCUSDT
                              - text: .
                          - listitem [ref=e3855]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3856]:
                              - text: Ou
                              - strong [ref=e3857]:
                                - code [ref=e3858]: ETHUSDT
                              - text: ", etc."
                      - listitem [ref=e3859]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e3860]:
                          - strong [ref=e3861]: SetBenchmark("BTCUSDT")
                        - list [ref=e3862]:
                          - listitem [ref=e3863]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3864]:
                              - text: Compare la performance de l’algorithme à l’évolution de
                              - strong [ref=e3865]: BTC
                              - text: .
                          - listitem [ref=e3866]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3867]: Vous pouvez changer par un autre benchmark (par ex. ETHUSDT) si souhaité.
                      - listitem [ref=e3868]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e3869]:
                          - strong [ref=e3870]: Brokerage
                        - list [ref=e3871]:
                          - listitem [ref=e3872]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3873]:
                              - code [ref=e3874]: SetBrokerageModel(BrokerageName.Binance, AccountType.Cash)
                              - text: permet d’indiquer à Lean d’utiliser la
                              - strong [ref=e3875]: simulation
                              - text: du brokerage Binance (frais, règles, etc.).
                          - listitem [ref=e3876]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3877]:
                              - text: Pour un
                              - strong [ref=e3878]: live trading
                              - text: réel, vous devez configurer vos
                              - strong [ref=e3879]: API keys
                              - text: et activer le brokerage live depuis l’IDE ou l’API.
                      - listitem [ref=e3880]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e3881]:
                          - strong [ref=e3882]: Taille des Positions
                        - list [ref=e3883]:
                          - listitem [ref=e3884]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3885]:
                              - code [ref=e3886]: _positionSize = 10;
                              - text: ": adapté à la crypto (selon la décimale de trading)."
                          - listitem [ref=e3887]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3888]: Ajustez à votre capital, risque, etc.
                      - listitem [ref=e3889]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e3890]:
                          - strong [ref=e3891]: Timeframes
                        - list [ref=e3892]:
                          - listitem [ref=e3893]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3894]:
                              - text: "On"
                              - strong [ref=e3895]: télécharge
                              - text: la paire en
                              - code [ref=e3896]: Resolution.Minute
                              - text: .
                          - listitem [ref=e3897]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3898]:
                              - text: On la
                              - strong [ref=e3899]: consolide
                              - text: en Daily/Horaire/5-Minutes.
                          - listitem [ref=e3900]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3901]: Vous pouvez changer les périodes, ex. 4h, 15m, etc.
                      - listitem [ref=e3902]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e3903]:
                          - strong [ref=e3904]: ZigZag Simplifié
                        - list [ref=e3905]:
                          - listitem [ref=e3906]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3907]:
                              - text: Comme dans les exemples précédents, c’est un
                              - strong [ref=e3908]: ZigZag “maison”
                              - text: rudimentaire.
                          - listitem [ref=e3909]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3910]:
                              - text: Si vous préférez, vous pouvez utiliser l’indicateur
                              - code [ref=e3911]: ZigZag
                              - text: natif de QuantConnect (dans
                              - strong [ref=e3912]:
                                - code [ref=e3913]: QuantConnect.Indicators
                              - text: ).
                          - listitem [ref=e3914]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3915]:
                              - text: Le
                              - code [ref=e3916]: ZigZagCanalDetector
                              - text: ici donne juste un squelette, vous pouvez l’enrichir (calculer un “IsBroken” qui compare la dernière barre aux bornes du canal, etc.).
                      - listitem [ref=e3917]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e3918]:
                          - strong [ref=e3919]: Trailing Stop & Double Take-Profit
                        - list [ref=e3920]:
                          - listitem [ref=e3921]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3922]: On relève le trailing stop en fonction du prix (pour un long).
                          - listitem [ref=e3923]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3924]:
                              - text: On effectue une prise de profit partielle (
                              - code [ref=e3925]: _takeProfit1
                              - text: ) puis une finale (
                              - code [ref=e3926]: _takeProfit2
                              - text: ).
                          - listitem [ref=e3927]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3928]:
                              - text: Les pourcentages (1%, 2%, etc.) sont
                              - strong [ref=e3929]: indicatifs
                              - text: . Ajustez selon la volatilité.
                      - listitem [ref=e3930]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e3931]:
                          - strong [ref=e3932]: Gestion du Risque
                        - list [ref=e3933]:
                          - listitem [ref=e3934]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3935]:
                              - text: Pensez à
                              - strong [ref=e3936]: backtester
                              - text: et à ajuster la taille de position (
                              - code [ref=e3937]: _positionSize
                              - text: ), le
                              - strong [ref=e3938]: stop
                              - text: ", etc."
                          - listitem [ref=e3939]:
                            - paragraph [ref=e3940]:
                              - text: Intégrer un
                              - strong [ref=e3941]: PositionSizing
                              - text: basé sur la volatilité (ex. ATR) pour ne pas prendre toujours la même taille.

                          - strong [ref=e3949]: Binance
                          - text: en
                          - strong [ref=e3950]: multi-timeframe
                          - text: (Daily/Horaire/5-Minutes).

                          - text: Utiliser un
                          - strong [ref=e3953]: ZigZag
                          - text: (simplifié) +
                          - strong [ref=e3954]: ADX
                          - text: pour filtrer la validité du canal.
                      - listitem [ref=e3955]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e3956]:
                          - text: Appliquer un
                          - strong [ref=e3957]: Trailing Stop
                          - text: +
                          - strong [ref=e3958]: Double TP
                          - text: .

                          - text: Définir
                          - strong [ref=e3961]: BTC
                          - text: comme
                          - strong [ref=e3962]: benchmark
                          - text: .

                      - text: Vous pouvez
                      - strong [ref=e3964]: personnaliser
                      - text: chaque brique (ZigZag, ADX, stops, etc.) et
                      - strong [ref=e3965]: remplacer
                      - text: la paire “BTUSDT” par toute
                      - strong [ref=e3966]: crypto
                      - text: réellement disponible dans l’univers Binance de QuantConnect. Bon trading !

// 0 => flat, 1 => long 1 BTC\\n\", \" decimal entryPrice = 0m;\\n\", \" decimal realizedPnL = 0m;\\n\", \"\\n\", \" foreach (var bar in hourlyBars.OrderBy(b => b.Time))\\n\", \" {\\n\", \" var hourPivot = hourPivotDict.ContainsKey(bar.Time) \\n\", \" ? hourPivotDict[bar.Time] \\n\", \" : PivotPointType.None;\\n\", \"\\n\", \" // daily key is bar.Time.Date\\n\", \" var dailyPivot = dailyPivotDict.ContainsKey(bar.Time.Date) \\n\", \" ? dailyPivotDict[bar.Time.Date] \\n\", \" : PivotPointType.None;\\n\", \"\\n\", \" // weekly key: we approximate the Monday of that week\\n\", \" var mondayOfWeek = GetWeekStartISO(bar.Time);\\n\", \" var weeklyPivot = weeklyPivotDict.ContainsKey(mondayOfWeek)\\n\", \" ? weeklyPivotDict[mondayOfWeek]\\n\", \" : PivotPointType.None;\\n\", \"\\n\", \" // condition for \\\"bullish alignment\\\"\\n\", \" bool bullish = (weeklyPivot == PivotPointType.Low) \\n\", \" && (dailyPivot == PivotPointType.Low) \\n\", \" && (hourPivot == PivotPointType.Low);\\n\", \"\\n\", \" // condition for \\\"bearish pivot\\\"\\n\", \" bool pivotIsBearish = (weeklyPivot == PivotPointType.High)\\n\", \" || (dailyPivot == PivotPointType.High)\\n\", \" || (hourPivot == PivotPointType.High);\\n\", \"\\n\", \" if (position == 0m && bullish)\\n\", \" {\\n\", \" // Enter long\\n\", \" position = 1m;\\n\", \" entryPrice = bar.Close;\\n\", \" }\\n\", \" else if (position > 0m && pivotIsBearish)\\n\", \" {\\n\", \" // Exit\\n\", \" realizedPnL += (bar.Close - entryPrice);                       - generic [ref=e4154]:
                        - text: "# Multi-Timeframe ZigZag Research (BTCUSDT on Binance)"
                        - text: "This notebook demonstrates a multi-timeframe approach using ZigZag indicators on:"
                        - text: "- **Weekly** (macro)"
                        - text: "- **Daily** (meso)"
                        - text: "- **Hourly** (micro)"
                        - text: "We then simulate a simple bullish-alignment strategy:"
                        - text: 1. When all ZigZags pivot to **Low** simultaneously, we go **long**.
                        - text: 2. Exit if any pivot flips to **High**.
                        - text: We'll see how the performance looks historically, and discuss ways to improve (like ADX filters, partial take-profit, or better threshold tuning).
                    - separator [ref=e4155]
                    - 'heading "Cell 2: Code – Imports & Basic Setup" [level=3] [ref=e4156]':
                      - strong [ref=e4157]: "Cell 2: Code – Imports & Basic Setup"
                    - generic [ref=e4165]:

                          - text: C#
                        - button "Copier" [ref=e4172] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - img [ref=e4173]
                      - generic [ref=e4179]:
                        - text: // C# environment references
                        - text: using QuantConnect;
                        - text: using QuantConnect.Data.Market;
                        - text: using QuantConnect.Data;
                        - text: using QuantConnect.Brokerages;
                        - text: using QuantConnect.Indicators;
                        - text: using System;
                        - text: using System.Linq;
                        - text: using System.Collections.Generic;
                        - text: using System.Globalization;
                        - text: using QuantConnect.Research;
                        - text: // Instantiate QuantBook
                        - text: var qb = new QuantBook();
                        - text: qb.SetAccountCurrency("USDT");
                        - text: qb.SetBrokerageModel(BrokerageName.Binance, AccountType.Cash);
                        - text: // Add the BTCUSDT pair (or any other) in Hour resolution
                        - text: var symbolBtcUsdt = qb.AddCrypto("BTCUSDT", Resolution.Hour, Market.Binance).Symbol;
                        - text: // Set date range
                        - text: var startDate = new DateTime(2013, 4, 7);
                        - text: var endDate = new DateTime(2024, 11, 1);
                        - text: // Fetch the Hourly data
                        - text: var btcHourBars = qb.History<TradeBar>(symbolBtcUsdt, startDate, endDate, Resolution.Hour).OrderBy(x => x.EndTime).ToList();
                        - text: "Console.WriteLine($\"Hourly bars retrieved: {btcHourBars.Count} rows\");"
                        - text: "Console.WriteLine($\"First bar: {btcHourBars.First().EndTime} O:{btcHourBars.First().Open} H:{btcHourBars.First().High} L:{btcHourBars.First().Low} C:{btcHourBars.First().Close}\");"
                        - text: "Console.WriteLine($\"Last bar: {btcHourBars.Last().EndTime} O:{btcHourBars.Last().Open} H:{btcHourBars.Last().High} L:{btcHourBars.Last().Low} C:{btcHourBars.Last().Close}\");"
                    - separator [ref=e4180]
                    - 'heading "Cell 3: Code – Aggregate Hourly to Daily & Weekly" [level=3] [ref=e4181]':
                      - strong [ref=e4182]: "Cell 3: Code – Aggregate Hourly to Daily & Weekly"
                    - generic [ref=e4190]:
                      - generic [ref=e4192]:
                        - generic [ref=e4193]:
                          - img [ref=e4194]
                          - text: C#
                        - button "Copier" [ref=e4197] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - img [ref=e4198]
                      - generic [ref=e4204]:
                        - text: // Convert Hourly -> Daily
                        - text: var dailyData = btcHourBars
                        - text: .GroupBy(x => x.EndTime.Date)
                        - text: .Select(g => new TradeBar
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: Time = g.Key,
                        - text: Open = g.First().Open,
                        - text: High = g.Max(x => x.High),
                        - text: Low = g.Min(x => x.Low),
                        - text: Close = g.Last().Close,
                        - text: Volume = g.Sum(x => x.Volume),
                        - text: Symbol = symbolBtcUsdt
                        - text: "})"
                        - text: .OrderBy(x => x.Time)
                        - text: .ToList();
                        - text: "Console.WriteLine($\"Daily bars: {dailyData.Count} rows, from {dailyData.First().Time} to {dailyData.Last().Time}\");"
                        - text: // Convert Daily -> Weekly
                        - text: var weeklyData = dailyData
                        - text: .GroupBy(bar => new
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: Year = bar.Time.Year,
                        - text: Week = CultureInfo.InvariantCulture.Calendar.GetWeekOfYear(
                        - text: bar.Time,
                        - text: CalendarWeekRule.FirstFourDayWeek,
                        - text: DayOfWeek.Monday)
                        - text: "})"
                        - text: .Select(g => new TradeBar
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: Time = g.Min(x => x.Time),
                        - text: Open = g.First().Open,
                        - text: High = g.Max(x => x.High),
                        - text: Low = g.Min(x => x.Low),
                        - text: Close = g.Last().Close,
                        - text: Volume = g.Sum(x => x.Volume),
                        - text: Symbol = symbolBtcUsdt
                        - text: "})"
                        - text: .OrderBy(x => x.Time)
                        - text: .ToList();
                        - text: "Console.WriteLine($\"Weekly bars: {weeklyData.Count} rows, from {weeklyData.First().Time} to {weeklyData.Last().Time}\");"
                    - separator [ref=e4205]
                    - 'heading "Cell 4: Code – ZigZag Setup & Pivot Dictionaries" [level=3] [ref=e4206]':
                      - strong [ref=e4207]: "Cell 4: Code – ZigZag Setup & Pivot Dictionaries"
                    - generic [ref=e4215]:
                      - generic [ref=e4217]:
                        - generic [ref=e4218]:
                          - img [ref=e4219]
                          - text: C#
                        - button "Copier" [ref=e4222] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - img [ref=e4223]
                      - generic [ref=e4229]:
                        - text: // We use ZigZag from Lean's Indicators namespace
                        - text: // We'll define a helper method to build a dictionary of (DateTime -> PivotPointType)
                        - text: Dictionary<DateTime, PivotPointType> BuildPivotDict(List<TradeBar> bars, decimal sensitivity, int minTrendLength)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: var pivotDict = new Dictionary<DateTime, PivotPointType>();
                        - text: var zigZag = new ZigZag("ZigZag", sensitivity, minTrendLength);
                        - text: foreach (var bar in bars.OrderBy(x => x.Time))
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: zigZag.Update(bar);
                        - text: // Pivot is only meaningful if IsReady
                        - text: if (zigZag.IsReady)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: pivotDict[bar.Time] = zigZag.PivotType;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: else
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: pivotDict[bar.Time] = PivotPointType.None;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: return pivotDict;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // Build pivot dictionaries for weekly, daily, hourly
                        - text: decimal sensitivity = 0.05m; // 5% threshold
                        - text: int minTrendLength = 2;
                        - text: var pivotWeekly = BuildPivotDict(weeklyData, sensitivity, minTrendLength);
                        - text: var pivotDaily = BuildPivotDict(dailyData, sensitivity, minTrendLength);
                        - text: var pivotHourly = BuildPivotDict(btcHourBars,sensitivity, minTrendLength);
                        - text: "Console.WriteLine($\"pivotWeekly: {pivotWeekly.Count} entries\");"
                        - text: "Console.WriteLine($\"pivotDaily: {pivotDaily.Count} entries\");"
                        - text: "Console.WriteLine($\"pivotHourly: {pivotHourly.Count} entries\");"
                    - separator [ref=e4230]
                    - 'heading "Cell 5: Code – Utility for Finding the Monday of a Week" [level=3] [ref=e4231]':
                      - strong [ref=e4232]: "Cell 5: Code – Utility for Finding the Monday of a Week"
                    - generic [ref=e4240]:
                      - generic [ref=e4242]:
                        - generic [ref=e4243]:
                          - img [ref=e4244]
                          - text: C#
                        - button "Copier" [ref=e4247] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - img [ref=e4248]
                      - generic [ref=e4254]:
                        - text: DateTime GetIsoWeekMonday(DateTime dt)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // Shift dt backward to the Monday of the same ISO week
                        - text: int delta = DayOfWeek.Monday - dt.DayOfWeek;
                        - text: if (delta > 0) delta -= 7;
                        - text: return dt.Date.AddDays(delta);
                        - text: "}"
                    - separator [ref=e4255]
                    - 'heading "Cell 6: Code – Simple Strategy Simulation" [level=3] [ref=e4256]':
                      - strong [ref=e4257]: "Cell 6: Code – Simple Strategy Simulation"
                    - generic [ref=e4265]:
                      - generic [ref=e4267]:
                        - generic [ref=e4268]:
                          - img [ref=e4269]
                          - text: C#
                        - button "Copier" [ref=e4272] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - img [ref=e4273]
                      - generic [ref=e4279]:
                        - text: /// <summary>
                        - text: "/// Performs a simple alignment strategy:"
                        - text: /// - If Weekly=Low, Daily=Low, Hourly=Low => Go long 1 BTC
                        - text: /// - If in position and we see a pivot High in any timeframe => exit
                        - text: /// - Realized PnL is tracked in BTC (you can multiply by bar.Close for USDT)
                        - text: /// </summary>
                        - text: void ZigZagAlignmentSim(
                        - text: List<TradeBar> hourBars,
                        - text: Dictionary<DateTime, PivotPointType> pivotWeekly,
                        - text: Dictionary<DateTime, PivotPointType> pivotDaily,
                        - text: Dictionary<DateTime, PivotPointType> pivotHour)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: decimal position = 0m; // 0 => no position, 1 => long 1 BTC
                        - text: decimal entryPrice = 0m;
                        - text: decimal realizedPnL = 0m;
                        - text: foreach (var bar in hourBars.OrderBy(x => x.Time))
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // Identify pivot for hourly
                        - text: var hourPivot = pivotHour.ContainsKey(bar.Time)
                        - text: "? pivotHour[bar.Time]"
                        - text: ": PivotPointType.None;"
                        - text: // Identify pivot for daily
                        - text: // daily key = bar.Time.Date
                        - text: var dayKey = bar.Time.Date;
                        - text: var dailyPivot = pivotDaily.ContainsKey(dayKey)
                        - text: "? pivotDaily[dayKey]"
                        - text: ": PivotPointType.None;"
                        - text: // Identify pivot for weekly
                        - text: var monday = GetIsoWeekMonday(bar.Time);
                        - text: var weeklyPivot = pivotWeekly.ContainsKey(monday)
                        - text: "? pivotWeekly[monday]"
                        - text: ": PivotPointType.None;"
                        - text: bool bullish = (weeklyPivot == PivotPointType.Low)
                        - text: "&& (dailyPivot == PivotPointType.Low)"
                        - text: "&& (hourPivot == PivotPointType.Low);"
                        - text: bool anyBearish = (weeklyPivot == PivotPointType.High)
                        - text: "|| (dailyPivot == PivotPointType.High)"
                        - text: "|| (hourPivot == PivotPointType.High);"
                        - text: if (position == 0m && bullish)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // enter long
                        - text: position = 1m;
                        - text: entryPrice = bar.Close;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: else if (position > 0m && anyBearish)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // exit
                        - text: realizedPnL += (bar.Close - entryPrice);
                        - text: position = 0m;
                        - text: entryPrice = 0m;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // close if still in position
                        - text: var lastBar = hourBars.Last();
                        - text: if (position > 0m)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: realizedPnL += (lastBar.Close - entryPrice);
                        - text: position = 0m;
                        - text: entryPrice = 0m;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "Console.WriteLine($\"[ZigZagAlignmentSim] Realized PnL in BTC: {realizedPnL:F4}\");"
                        - text: "Console.WriteLine($\"If you prefer USDT, multiply by last price {lastBar.Close} => {realizedPnL * lastBar.Close:F2} USDT\");"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // Run the simulation
                        - text: ZigZagAlignmentSim(btcHourBars, pivotWeekly, pivotDaily, pivotHourly);
                    - separator [ref=e4280]
                    - 'heading "Cell 7: Markdown – Discussion & Next Steps" [level=3] [ref=e4281]':
                      - strong [ref=e4282]: "Cell 7: Markdown – Discussion & Next Steps"
                    - generic [ref=e4290]:
                      - generic [ref=e4292]:
                        - generic [ref=e4293]:
                          - img [ref=e4294]
                          - text: Markdown
                        - button "Copier" [ref=e4297] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - img [ref=e4298]
                      - generic [ref=e4304]:
                        - text: "# Discussion"
                        - text: "- **Negative or Low PnL**: It's possible this simple approach underperforms because it's very restrictive."
                        - text: "- **Possible Improvements**:"
                        - text: "1. **ADX Filter**: Only trade when the ADX in each timeframe is above a threshold, indicating stronger trends."
                        - text: "2. **Partial Profit / Trailing Stop**: Instead of holding 1 BTC until a pivot flips, gradually take profits or raise a trailing stop."
                        - text: "3. **Parameter Tuning**: The `sensitivity = 0.05m` might be too high or too low. Experiment with 2–3% or 10% to see if there's a better match for BTC's volatility."
                        - text: "4. **Visual Validation**: Plot some portion of the data (e.g., last 1 year) with pivot labels to confirm the alignment logic is correct."
                        - text: "5. **Short Selling**: You can also add conditions for short entries when all pivots are `High`."
                        - text: "6. **Robustness**: Add a `StopLoss` in percentage terms, or combine the pivot approach with a simple moving average filter."
                        - text: "Finally, you might compare your results to:"
                        - text: "- A simple HODL benchmark (holding BTC from the start)."
                        - text: "- Alternative rules (like trading only if Weekly and Daily are the same, ignoring Hourly)."
                        - text: This concludes the improved structure of the notebook.

dt.DayOfWeek;\\n\", \" if (delta > 0) delta -= 7;\\n\", \" return dt.Date.AddDays(delta);\\n\", \"}\\n\", \"\\n\", \"/// <summary>\\n\", \"/// Hypothetical trading sim:\\n\", \"/// - If (Weekly=Low && Daily=Low && Hour=Low) => go long if we're not in position\\n\", \"/// - If any pivot flips to High => exit\\n\", \"/// We'll store the PnL by buying 1 BTC (very simplistic).\\n\", \"/// </summary>\\n\", \"void SimpleZigZagSim(\\n\", \" List<TradeBar> hourlyBars, \\n\", \" Dictionary<DateTime, PivotPointType> weeklyPivotDict,\\n\", \" Dictionary<DateTime, PivotPointType> dailyPivotDict,\\n\", \" Dictionary<DateTime, PivotPointType> hourPivotDict)\\n\", \"{\\n\", \" decimal position = 0m; // 0 => flat, 1 => long 1 BTC\\n\", \" decimal entryPrice = 0m;\\n\", \" decimal realizedPnL = 0m;\\n\", \"\\n\", \" foreach (var bar in hourlyBars.OrderBy(b => b.Time))\\n\", \" {\\n\", \" var hourPivot = hourPivotDict.ContainsKey(bar.Time) \\n\", \" ? hourPivotDict[bar.Time] \\n\", \" : PivotPointType.None;\\n\", \"\\n\", \" // daily key is bar.Time.Date\\n\", \" var dailyPivot = dailyPivotDict.ContainsKey(bar.Time.Date) \\n\", \" ? dailyPivotDict[bar.Time.Date] \\n\", \" : PivotPointType.None;\\n\", \"\\n\", \" // weekly key: we approximate the Monday of that week\\n\", \" var mondayOfWeek = GetWeekStartISO(bar.Time);\\n\", \" var weeklyPivot = weeklyPivotDict.ContainsKey(mondayOfWeek)\\n\", \" ? weeklyPivotDict[mondayOfWeek]\\n\", \" : PivotPointType.None;\\n\", \"\\n\", \" // condition for \\\"bullish alignment\\\"\\n\", \" bool bullish = (weeklyPivot == PivotPointType.Low) \\n\", \" && (dailyPivot == PivotPointType.Low) \\n\", \" && (hourPivot == PivotPointType.Low);\\n\", \"\\n\", \" // condition for \\\"bearish pivot\\\"\\n\", \" bool pivotIsBearish = (weeklyPivot == PivotPointType.High)\\n\", \" || (dailyPivot == PivotPointType.High)\\n\", \" || (hourPivot == PivotPointType.High);\\n\", \"\\n\", \" if (position == 0m && bullish)\\n\", \" {\\n\", \" // Enter long\\n\", \" position = 1m;\\n\", \" entryPrice = bar.Close;\\n\", \" }\\n\", \" else if (position > 0m && pivotIsBearish)\\n\", \" {\\n\", \" // Exit\\n\", \" realizedPnL += (bar.Close - entryPrice); \\n\", \" position = 0m;\\n\", \" entryPrice = 0m;\\n\", \" }\\n\", \" }\\n\", \"\\n\", \" // If we end still in position, let's close at last bar\\n\", \" var lastBar = hourlyBars.Last();\\n\", \" if (position > 0m)\\n\", \" {\\n\", \" realizedPnL += (lastBar.Close -                       - generic [ref=e4401]:
                        - text: "## Plotting Daily Bars with ZigZag Pivots (Plotly.NET)"
                        - text: "In this section, we will:"
                        - text: 1. Create a line chart of daily BTCUSDT bars (Close price).
                        - text: 2. Highlight pivot points (PivotPointType.High vs. PivotPointType.Low) with separate scatter traces.
                        - text: 3. Display the chart directly in the notebook.
                        - text: "**Note:**"
                        - text: "- Make sure you have the Plotly.NET library available in your environment (it usually comes with QuantConnect’s research environment)."
                        - text: "- We will color pivot lows in green and pivot highs in red."
                    - heading "1.2 C# Code" [level=3] [ref=e4402]

                      - generic [ref=e4424]:
                        - text: ////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
                        - text: //
                        - text: // 1) VISUALIZE DAILY BARS AND ZIGZAG PIVOTS
                        - text: //
                        - text: ////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
                        - text: // 1A) Ensure we have Plotly.NET references
                        - text: using Plotly.NET;
                        - text: using Plotly.NET.LayoutObjects;
                        - text: using System.Drawing;
                        - text: /// <summary>
                        - text: /// Prepares a chart with daily close line + pivot markers.
                        - text: /// </summary>
                        - text: GenericChart.GenericChart PlotDailyWithPivots(
                        - text: List<TradeBar> dailyBars,
                        - text: Dictionary<DateTime, PivotPointType> dailyPivotDict
                        - text: )
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // Sort bars by date
                        - text: var sorted = dailyBars.OrderBy(b => b.Time).ToList();
                        - text: "// X-axis: DateTime"
                        - text: var xDates = sorted.Select(b => b.Time).ToList();
                        - text: "// Y-axis: daily close prices"
                        - text: var yClose = sorted.Select(b => (double)b.Close).ToList();
                        - text: // 1) Main line chart (close)
                        - text: var closeTrace = Chart2D.Line<DateTime, double, string>(
                        - text: "x: xDates,"
                        - text: "y: yClose,"
                        - text: "Name: \"Daily Close\""
                        - text: );
                        - text: // 2) Build arrays for pivot highs vs. pivot lows
                        - text: var pivotHighXs = new List<DateTime>();
                        - text: var pivotHighYs = new List<double>();
                        - text: var pivotLowXs = new List<DateTime>();
                        - text: var pivotLowYs = new List<double>();
                        - text: foreach (var bar in sorted)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: var pivot = dailyPivotDict.ContainsKey(bar.Time)
                        - text: "? dailyPivotDict[bar.Time]"
                        - text: ": PivotPointType.None;"
                        - text: if (pivot == PivotPointType.High)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: pivotHighXs.Add(bar.Time);
                        - text: pivotHighYs.Add((double)bar.Close);
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: else if (pivot == PivotPointType.Low)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: pivotLowXs.Add(bar.Time);
                        - text: pivotLowYs.Add((double)bar.Close);
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // 3) Scatter for pivot highs (red)
                        - text: var pivotHighTrace = Chart2D.Scatter<DateTime, double, string>(
                        - text: "x: pivotHighXs,"
                        - text: "y: pivotHighYs,"
                        - text: "mode: StyleParam.Mode.Markers,"
                        - text: "Name: \"Pivot High\","
                        - text: "marker: new Plotly.NET.Marker"
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: Color = Color.Red,
                        - text: Size = 6
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: );
                        - text: // 4) Scatter for pivot lows (green)
                        - text: var pivotLowTrace = Chart2D.Scatter<DateTime, double, string>(
                        - text: "x: pivotLowXs,"
                        - text: "y: pivotLowYs,"
                        - text: "mode: StyleParam.Mode.Markers,"
                        - text: "Name: \"Pivot Low\","
                        - text: "marker: new Plotly.NET.Marker"
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: Color = Color.Green,
                        - text: Size = 6
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: );
                        - text: // Combine all
                        - text: var combinedChart = Chart.Combine(
                        - text: new GenericChart.GenericChart[]
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: closeTrace,
                        - text: pivotHighTrace,
                        - text: pivotLowTrace
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: );
                        - text: return combinedChart;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "// Now let's create and display the chart for our `dailyData` and `dailyPivotDict`:"
                        - text: var dailyChart = PlotDailyWithPivots(dailyData, dailyPivotDict);
                        - text: // Display the chart in the notebook
                        - text: Display(dailyChart);

                    - 'heading "2) Improved Strategy Example: Partial Exit + Trailing Stop" [level=2] [ref=e4435]'
                    - heading "2.1 Markdown Explanation" [level=3] [ref=e4436]
                    - generic [ref=e4444]:
                      - generic [ref=e4446]:
                        - generic [ref=e4447]:

                        - button "Copier" [ref=e4451] [cursor=pointer]:

                      - generic [ref=e4458]:
                        - text: "## Improved ZigZag Strategy (Partial Exits & Trailing Stop)"
                        - text: "We update our simple long/flat approach to:"
                        - text: "1. **Enter** long if weekly/daily/hourly all align with `Low` pivot."
                        - text: 2. **Use** a trailing stop that increments upward (for long positions).
                        - text: "3. **Sell half** at a modest profit target (e.g., +3%), then hold the remainder until:"
                        - text: "- Another pivot flips to `High`, or"
                        - text: "- The trailing stop is triggered."
                        - text: 4. **Close** any remaining position at final bar.
                        - text: This can help lock in partial gains and reduce drawdowns when the market reverses.
                    - heading "2.2 C# Code" [level=3] [ref=e4459]
                    - generic [ref=e4467]:
                      - generic [ref=e4469]:
                        - generic [ref=e4470]:
                          - img [ref=e4471]
                          - text: C#
                        - button "Copier" [ref=e4474] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - img [ref=e4475]
                      - generic [ref=e4481]:
                        - text: ////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
                        - text: //
                        - text: // 2) IMPROVED STRATEGY EXAMPLE
                        - text: //
                        - text: ////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
                        - text: void ZigZagStrategy_PartialExitAndTrailingStop(
                        - text: List<TradeBar> hourBars,
                        - text: Dictionary<DateTime, PivotPointType> pivotWeekly,
                        - text: Dictionary<DateTime, PivotPointType> pivotDaily,
                        - text: Dictionary<DateTime, PivotPointType> pivotHour,
                        - text: decimal profitTargetPercent = 0.03m, // 3% partial take-profit
                        - text: decimal trailingStopPercent = 0.02m // 2% trailing stop from highest close
                        - text: )
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: decimal position = 0m; // 0 => no position, 1 => long 1 BTC
                        - text: decimal entryPrice = 0m; // entry fill price
                        - text: decimal realizedPnL = 0m; // total PnL in BTC
                        - text: bool partialTaken = false; // did we already take half?
                        - text: decimal peakPrice = 0m; // track the highest close while in position
                        - text: foreach (var bar in hourBars.OrderBy(x => x.Time))
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // Identify pivot for hourly
                        - text: "var hourPivot = pivotHour.ContainsKey(bar.Time) ? pivotHour[bar.Time] : PivotPointType.None;"
                        - text: // Identify pivot for daily
                        - text: var dailyPivot = pivotDaily.ContainsKey(bar.Time.Date)
                        - text: "? pivotDaily[bar.Time.Date]"
                        - text: ": PivotPointType.None;"
                        - text: // Identify pivot for weekly
                        - text: var monday = GetIsoWeekMonday(bar.Time);
                        - text: var weeklyPivot = pivotWeekly.ContainsKey(monday)
                        - text: "? pivotWeekly[monday]"
                        - text: ": PivotPointType.None;"
                        - text: bool bullish = (weeklyPivot == PivotPointType.Low)
                        - text: "&& (dailyPivot == PivotPointType.Low)"
                        - text: "&& (hourPivot == PivotPointType.Low);"
                        - text: bool anyBearish = (weeklyPivot == PivotPointType.High)
                        - text: "|| (dailyPivot == PivotPointType.High)"
                        - text: "|| (hourPivot == PivotPointType.High);"
                        - text: // If no position and bullish => enter
                        - text: if (position == 0m && bullish)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: position = 1m;
                        - text: entryPrice = bar.Close;
                        - text: peakPrice = bar.Close; // initialize peak
                        - text: partialTaken = false;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // If in position, check for trailing stop, partial exit, or pivot-based exit
                        - text: else if (position > 0m)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // Update peak
                        - text: if (bar.Close > peakPrice) peakPrice = bar.Close;
                        - text: // 1) Trailing Stop => if close < (peakPrice * (1 - trailingStopPercent)), exit all
                        - text: decimal stopPrice = peakPrice * (1m - trailingStopPercent);
                        - text: if (bar.Close < stopPrice)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: realizedPnL += (bar.Close - entryPrice);
                        - text: position = 0m;
                        - text: entryPrice = 0m;
                        - text: peakPrice = 0m;
                        - text: partialTaken = false;
                        - text: continue;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // 2) Partial exit => if close >= (entryPrice * (1 + profitTargetPercent)) and partial not taken
                        - text: decimal partialPrice = entryPrice * (1m + profitTargetPercent);
                        - text: if (!partialTaken && bar.Close >= partialPrice)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: // Sell half => 0.5 BTC
                        - text: realizedPnL += 0.5m * (bar.Close - entryPrice);
                        - text: // We remain with 0.5 BTC at an average cost basis => do a simplistic approach
                        - text: // We'll treat the position as still "1 BTC" for simplicity,
                        - text: // but keep in mind we've locked in half the profit.
                        - text: partialTaken = true;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // 3) Pivot-based exit => if any pivot flips to High
                        - text: if (anyBearish)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: realizedPnL += (bar.Close - entryPrice);
                        - text: position = 0m;
                        - text: entryPrice = 0m;
                        - text: peakPrice = 0m;
                        - text: partialTaken = false;
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: // If still in position at the end, close
                        - text: var lastBar = hourBars.Last();
                        - text: if (position > 0m)
                        - text: "{"
                        - text: realizedPnL += (lastBar.Close - entryPrice);
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "Console.WriteLine($\"[PartialExitStrategy] Final PnL(BTC): {realizedPnL:F4}\");"
                        - text: "Console.WriteLine($\"Equivalent in USDT at {lastBar.Close} => {(realizedPnL * lastBar.Close):F2}\");"
                        - text: "}"
                        - text: "// Let's run the improved strategy:"
                        - text: ZigZagStrategy_PartialExitAndTrailingStop(
                        - text: "hourBars: btcHourBars,"
                        - text: "pivotWeekly: pivotWeekly,"
                        - text: "pivotDaily: pivotDaily,"
                        - text: "pivotHour: pivotHourly,"
                        - text: "profitTargetPercent: 0.03m, // e.g. 3%"
                        - text: "trailingStopPercent: 0.02m // e.g. 2% trailing stop"
                        - text: );
                    - paragraph [ref=e4482]:
                      - strong [ref=e4483]: "Discussion:"
                    - list [ref=e4484]:
                      - listitem [ref=e4485]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e4486]: This method might still yield a negative result depending on data and thresholds.
                      - listitem [ref=e4487]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e4488]:
                          - text: You can adjust
                          - code [ref=e4489]: profitTargetPercent
                          - text: and
                          - code [ref=e4490]: trailingStopPercent
                          - text: for better outcomes.
                      - listitem [ref=e4491]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e4492]:
                          - text: Incorporate an
                          - strong [ref=e4493]: ADX filter
                          - text: or
                          - strong [ref=e4494]: RSI
                          - text: filter to skip trades in choppy markets if needed.
                    - separator [ref=e4495]
                    - heading "3) Additional Notes" [level=3] [ref=e4496]
                    - list [ref=e4497]:
                      - listitem [ref=e4498]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e4499]:
                          - strong [ref=e4500]: Plotly.NET
                          - text: "usage: if the chart does not display, ensure your environment supports it. In some cases, you might need"
                          - code [ref=e4501]: DisplayHTML(chart.ToKATEX())
                          - text: or similar.
                      - listitem [ref=e4502]:
                        - paragraph [ref=e4503]:
                          - strong [ref=e4504]: Parameter Tuning
                          - text: ":"
                        - list [ref=e4505]:

                            - paragraph [ref=e4507]:
                              - text: The
                              - code [ref=e4508]: ZigZag
                              - text: sensitivity might need to be higher or lower for crypto.
                          - listitem [ref=e4509]:

                      - listitem [ref=e4511]:

                          - text: ": you can easily add logic for short entries if weekly/daily/hourly all pivot"

\"metadata\": {}, \"outputs\": [], \"source\": [ \"import pandas as pd\\n\", \"import numpy as np\\n\", \"\\n\", \"def classic_chart_zigzag(df, thresholdPercent=0.05):\\n\", \" \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n\", \" Manually computes ZigZag pivots in the style of typical charting platforms.\\n\", \" df must have columns 'time' and 'close'.\\n\", \" thresholdPercent=0.05 => 5% retracement needed to lock in a pivot.\\n\", \"\\n\", \" Returns a list of pivots: (time, price, +1 or -1) \\n\", \" +1 => Low pivot\\n\", \" -1 => High pivot\\n\", \" \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n\", \" if len(df) < 2:\\n\", \" return []\\n\", \"\\n\", \" # We'll store (time, price, sign)\\n\", \" pivots = []\\n\", \"\\n\", \" # 1) Start with the first bar as pivot\\n\", \" firstBar = df.iloc[0]\\n\", \" lastPivotPrice = firstBar['close']\\n\", \" lastPivotTime = firstBar['time']\\n\", \"\\n\", \" # 2) Determine initial direction (up or down) by comparing the second bar\\n\", \" secondBar = df.iloc[1]\\n\", \" directionUp = secondBar['close'] > lastPivotPrice # True => up, False => down\\n\", \"\\n\", \" # If directionUp => we want to find new \\\"high extremes\\\"\\n\", \" # If directionUp=False => we want to find new \\\"low extremes\\\"\\n\", \"\\n\", \" # Track the extreme in the current direction\\n\", \" currentExtremePrice = lastPivotPrice\\n\", \" currentExtremeTime = lastPivotTime\\n\", \"\\n\", \" # We record the sign for the first pivot:\\n\", \" # if directionUp => first pivot is a Low (+1)\\n\", \" # else => first pivot is a High (-1)\\n\", \" lastSign = +1 if directionUp else -1\\n\", \"\\n\", \" # We'll add that initial pivot to the list\\n\", \" pivots.append((lastPivotTime, lastPivotPrice, lastSign))\\n\", \"\\n\", \" for i in range(1, len(df)):\\n\", \" row = df.iloc[i]\\n\", \" price = row['close']\\n\", \" time = row['time']\\n\", \"\\n\", \" # Update extremes in the current direction\\n\", \" if directionUp:\\n\", \" # If price is higher than currentExtreme => update extreme\\n\", \" if price > currentExtremePrice:\\n\", \" currentExtremePrice = price\\n\", \" currentExtremeTime = time\\n\", \" else:\\n\", \" # Check if we retraced enough to confirm a new pivot\\n\", \" retrace = 1.0 - (price / currentExtremePrice)\\n\", \" if retrace >= thresholdPercent:\\n\", \" # That means we lock in the old extreme as a High pivot\\n\", \" # Switch direction to down\\n\", \" pivots.append((currentExtremeTime, currentExtremePrice, -1))\\n\", \"\\n\", \" # Now the new pivot is the current bar as \\\"low start\\\"\\n\", \" directionUp = False\\n\", \" currentExtremePrice = price\\n\", \" currentExtremeTime = time\\n\", \" else:\\n\", \" # directionDown => track new low extremes\\n\", \" if price < currentExtremePrice:\\n\", \" currentExtremePrice = price\\n\", \" currentExtremeTime = time\\n\", \" else:\\n\", \" # Check if we rallied enough to confirm a new pivot\\n\", \" rally = (price / currentExtremePrice) - 1.0\\n\", \" if rally >= thresholdPercent:\\n\", \" # Lock in the old extreme as a Low pivot\\n\", \" pivots.append((currentExtremeTime, currentExtremePrice, +1))\\n\", \"\\n\", \" directionUp = True\\n\", \" currentExtremePrice = price\\n\", \" currentExtremeTime = time\\n\", \"\\n\", \" # The last extreme can be appended as the final pivot if you want\\n\", \" # e.g., treat the last bar as a pivot if you prefer\\n\", \" finalPrice = currentExtremePrice\\n\", \" finalTime = currentExtremeTime\\n\", \" finalSign = +1 if not directionUp else -1 # Because if we ended going up, the last pivot is High\\n\", \" pivots.append((finalTime, finalPrice, finalSign))\\n\", \"\\n\", \" # Now we have a strictly alternating pivot list\\n\", \" return pivots\\n\", \"\\n\", \"pivotList = classic_chart_zigzag(bars_df[['time','close']], thresholdPercent=0.05)\\n\" ] }, { \"cell_type\": \"markdown\", \"metadata\": {}, \"source\": [ \"## Plotting the ZigZag Indicator\\n\", \"\\n\", \"We
